< Review>
Facilmente es la mejor comida Mexica autentica en Los Angeles, and I've tried so many places. Their menu is delicious and has something for everyone, and their taste is consistent every single time. Absolutely love their salsas! If you are into spicy, this is your place.The service from the owners and their family makes it such an enjoyable experience, they have a great attitude. Prices are more than fair. Try anything on their menu and you'll be blown away from the authenticity, freshness, and taste.< /Review>

< Review>
Where do I start... this place is out of this world!! To start off, this is 110% AUTHENTIC MEXICAN cuisine. I've had almost their entire menu and everything is delicious! Some of my favorites: tortas ahogadas, carne en su jugo, queso fundido,chilaquiles, and thwir salsas are soo tasty, spicy, and all have a different kick! The owners are so down-to-earth, professional, and genuine. Everything about this gem is a VIBE.. the place's deco is super cute, the food is amazing, and their service is great! Check them out, you'll wish you had done it sooner!< /Review>

<Time>1582234548361<//Time><rating>5< /rating>< review>
Updated again. Updated! This is my brother in law's place. I live in another state but have enjoyed his cooking for many years! You definitely need to visit and you will taste authentic flavors straight out of Mexico.  I cant wait to go myself.
Later.... my wife arrived from Los Angeles with a Torta Ahogada from this place. Can you believe? First bite was Awesome... same as ever.
Finally, actually went there 11Mayo2019. Menu is more than i expected. Food is better than i remember. This is an undiscovered gem! They are planning to add outside tables under the trees in a rear courtyard.
Another visit, another great experience.  Agua de Jamica is the best i have ever had, full of flavor and slightly tart, not sticky sweet like most places. You gotta try this place yourself.

Here again today. Was here 3 days ago. Torta ahogada mojada was even better than  before. Approaching addiction.

Son in law likes mixing Jarritos Tamarindo with Agua Jamaica.

Just back from Guadalajara, ate in 3 popular restaurants, AND Carnes Asadas Pancho Lopez in Los Angeles still has the best tasting Torta Ahogada!

Now with live music!< /review>

< review>
I went in to have my hair colored with henna. Usually I do it myself but I thought I'd try them since they're just down the street from my house, right next door to where I buy henna. The person who did my hair was nice and proficient. The lady who I'm assuming it's the owner checked on her frequently like she was in training or something. The place was clean which I appreciated.

What got me irritated is after the service they advertise as $30 I was told would be $45 because of my hair length. This wasn't discussed beforehand. Also my hair comes past my shoulders but not to the middle of my back. When I pointed out to the owner that my hair was the same length as hers she said, "Well I have fine hair. Yours is thicker."  She hadn't even touched my hair!

And I completely understand charging more if more work is required but there should have been a discussion beforehand and I know it only costs me about $6 to buy the henna I need for my hair. I've also been to another shop and had it done before for less. She wanted to get over on me but I know it should not cost $50 (including tip) to get my hair colored only. No wash or anything. They only put the henna in. I had to wash it out myself.

No thank you!<//review>

< Review>
I needed a tire patch and alignment. I was promptly greeted in the parking lot by a friendly employee. The alignment price was about the same as competitor prices but the patch was free.  All the employees were friendly and seemed genuinely happy to have my business. They have 8 service bays.   Four  in the front and four in the back.  This location just opened last week as of this posting. They had coffee and popcorn as well as vending machines.   There's also a Wendy's in the parking lot if you need a bite to eat if waiting for your vehicle.  All tire shops try to upsell but these guys were not pushy at all.  They're just doing their job. I'll definitely be back.< /Review>

I worked with Patrick Hawkins and Jon Dodart on a claim - they teamed up together beautifully, and got me significantly more than I was expecting in a settlement at our deposition. These are both professionals that you want on your side when you are dealing with a system as complex, bureaucratic and unfriendly as the California comp system.   I would strongly advise against trying to navigate the system on your own - there are too many nuances and traps that liability insurers will try to lure you into and then use against you.  It‚Äôs reassuring to have a team that is always available to advise as the process unfolds - for instance, when someone shows up at your door and wants to take a recorded statement and have you sign away permission for them to access ALL your medical records, it‚Äôs unsettling and can be intimidating, especially when they are positioning it not as an ask but as a requirement.  Patrick and Jon were able to talk me through the situation and assure me that I wasn‚Äôt obligated to give them any information (and they subsequently made sure that all communication went through them).

They both were sensitive to what I felt what was in my best interest   - they were willing to try to settle before the deposition because I didn‚Äôt want this to drag on, but advised that settlements often happen quickly if you show up.  Patrick set everything up from his office, and Jon showed up and walked me through what to expect.  Before I knew it, he and the opposing lawyer had secured a settlement twice as high as I expected - Jon advised me the pros and cons of taking the settlement, and I knew quickly that this the best scenario given how timeI-intensive a case would be.  Because I had been set up so well and hadn‚Äôt given anything away early on to be used against me thanks to Jon and Patrick‚Äôs guidance, we were in a great position. I signed some paperwork that Jon scrupulously reviewed, and got a check a month or so later.

Again - don‚Äôt try to do this on your own.  The reduced stress and the likely increased settlement that comes from having such an experienced and helpful team on your side is well worth the contingency.</Text>

I was able to call first and get a free consultation on what would happen if I wanted to this firm to represent me and my workers comp case. This gave me a sense of relief and actually over time proved to be totally worth it. I was provided with therapies, medications, and doctors visits almost every week. <UserId.>101609980551837695684< /UserId.>< Response>
None<//Response>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Mezcal grill is definitely a little more catered to "American" tastes than other options nearby, but mostly in terms of the decor. Their menu has a lot of classic Mexican dishes, including mole, regular and "street" style tacos, and a whole bunch of other stuff that looks great. I usually stick to the burritos though, both because I'm poor and the main plates are a little pricey, and the burritos have never disappointed. They never go too heavy on the seasonings, if anything it tastes lighter than most other burritos, if that makes sense, the flavors are well balanced, and I've never had a messy burrito (no one wants a messy burrito).  They have a good variety of salsas, but I've never gone for any other than the standard pico de gallo and green stuff (I gotta figure out what it's called) because they're outstanding on chips and as a garnish on whatever you're eating.  This place is my go-to for all of the above reasons.< /Review>

<rating>4<//rating><Review>Came here for a birthday dinner. It's somewhere in between one of those casual Mexican restaurants where you order at the counter and get to enjoy all the delights of the salsa and chips bar, and a full blown fancy restaurant where your every whim is catered to. This place has a bit of an upper crust look, and it tries to travel in the same direction with it's fancy menu as well. This was perfect for a birthday celebration feel. I tried the Chile relleno plate, my husband got something with shrimp, and my mother in law got the nachos. The nachos were loaded, no doubt. I didn't try the shrimp plate but my husband said it was good. The Chile relleno was as I expected -- the truth is I have to realize I'm just not much for the blandness of the Chile relleno plate where bite after bite is the same. It's not that I don't like chili. I do. I love spicy peppers. It's just... Like I said, you take one bite, you have taken them now. Now let me say though that it was coated in a delicious red sauce. However.... It was fully coated. So it left no difference for comparisons. The waiter who assisted us was very nice and pleasant and attentive to refilling our drinks. We brought our little one with us also and the restaurant was very accommodating. Overall a pleasant experience, but perhaps should have tried a super burrito or their tacos instead.<//Review>< Pics>

<UserId.>102611543188847493079<//UserId.>< user_name>
Doug Berwick</user_name>
< rating>
5< /rating>
<pics>None< /pics><time>1514479763306< /time>< Review>
Excellent food. I work close to this restaurant, so coming here often is easy for me. It has a lot of good food, and I've spent time ordering a lot of different things on the (continuously improving) menu to get a really good idea of the food variety they have to offer here.

They have great meats here, my favorite probably being the chile verde. I love that you can get it in a burrito! That's a standard order of mine. Lately I've been branching out and getting crispy tacos with al pastor, carnitas, carne asada, etc. They're all great. They have outstanding shrimp tacos as well, that have a bit of spice mixed in. A wonderful tomato-based sauce goes with 3-4 large shrimp in each taco.

The salsa bar is pretty good, and while I like spicy foods, the flavor of the mild salsas here are better, for me, than the spicy varieties.

The rice and beans you get with meal plates are standard. They're not amazingly special by any means, but they give you what you're looking for when you get rice and beans: carb-y bites of nicely-done rice with creamy refried beans, and a touch of cotija on top. Standard, and good.

Yes, I'd recommend this place.<//Review>

<Text>You know it's a great taqueria with great food when everyone inside is Latino cheering on the soccer game.

When the food came, I knew I was spot on. I ordered the super nachos with carne asada and taco salad with carnitas. The portions were more than enough even if you come in starving and they are generous with the meats. They use romaine lettuce rather than iceberg like most other taquerias so that was a plus. They also have a chips and salsa bar that you can help yourself to. The avocado salsa was simply amazing! I repeat, amazing! Much thicker and creamier than I've had elsewhere and even had chucks of real avocado still in there.

If I didn't live so far from this place, I would be a regular.< /Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>
